        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
            document.querySelectorAll(".slider").forEach(function(slider) {
                var slides = slider.querySelector(".slides");
                var images = slider.querySelectorAll(".slides img");
                var prevBtn = slider.querySelector(".prev");
                var nextBtn = slider.querySelector(".next");

                var index = 0;

                // Set the slides container width based on the number of images
                slides.style.width = images.length * 100 + "%";

                // Show the correct slide
                function showSlide(i) {
                    index = (i + images.length) % images.length; // Wrap index
                    slides.style.transform = "translateX(-" + (index * 100 / images.length) + "%)";
                }

                function nextSlide() {
                    showSlide(index + 1);
                }

                function prevSlide() {
                    showSlide(index - 1);
                }

                // Add event listeners for navigation buttons
                if (prevBtn) prevBtn.addEventListener("click", prevSlide);
                if (nextBtn) nextBtn.addEventListener("click", nextSlide);

                // Responsive behavior: Adjust slides on window resize
                window.addEventListener("resize", function () {
                    showSlide(index); // Recalculate position
                });
            });
        });

(function(){
  var conf = window.WDW_POPUP_CONF || {};
  var SHOW_DELAY_MS = Number(conf.SHOW_DELAY_MS || 1500);
  var SUPPRESS_DAYS = Number(conf.SUPPRESS_DAYS || 7);
  var SHOW_FLOAT    = !!conf.SHOW_FLOAT;

  var STORAGE_KEY = "wdwPopupDismissedAt";
  var BODY_OPEN_CLASS = "wdw-popup-open";

  function daysSince(ts){ return (Date.now() - ts) / (1000*60*60*24); }
  function shouldSuppress(){
    try{ var ts = Number(localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY)); return ts && daysSince(ts) < SUPPRESS_DAYS; }
    catch(e){ return false; }
  }
  function setSuppress(){ try{ localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, String(Date.now())); }catch(e){} }

  // Scroll lock that restores previous values
  var prevOverflowHtml = '';
  var prevOverflowBody = '';
  function lockScroll(lock){
    if(lock){
      prevOverflowHtml = document.documentElement.style.overflow;
      prevOverflowBody = document.body.style.overflow;
      document.documentElement.style.overflow = 'hidden';
      document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    } else {
      document.documentElement.style.overflow = (prevOverflowHtml != null ? prevOverflowHtml : '');
      document.body.style.overflow = (prevOverflowBody != null ? prevOverflowBody : '');
    }
  }

  // Build popup DOM fresh each open; remove entirely on close
  function buildPopup(){
    var frag = document.createDocumentFragment();

    var backdrop = document.createElement('div');
    backdrop.id = 'wdwBackdrop';
    backdrop.className = 'wdw-backdrop';
    frag.appendChild(backdrop);

    var modal = document.createElement('div');
    modal.id = 'wdwModal';
    modal.className = 'wdw-modal';
    frag.appendChild(modal);

    var card = document.createElement('div');
    card.className = 'wdw-card';
    card.setAttribute('role','dialog');
    card.setAttribute('aria-modal','true');
    card.setAttribute('tabindex','-1');
    card.setAttribute('aria-labelledby','wdwHeading');

    // Close (SVG)
    var closeBtn = document.createElement('button');
    closeBtn.className = 'wdw-close';
    closeBtn.id = 'wdwClose';
    closeBtn.setAttribute('aria-label','Close');

    var svgNS = 'http://www.w3.org/2000/svg';
    var svg = document.createElementNS(svgNS, 'svg');
    svg.setAttribute('viewBox', '0 0 24 24');
    var path = document.createElementNS(svgNS, 'path');
    path.setAttribute('d', 'M18.3 5.71a1 1 0 0 0-1.41 0L12 10.59 7.11 5.7A1 1 0 1 0 5.7 7.11L10.59 12l-4.9 4.89a1 1 0 1 0 1.41 1.41L12 13.41l4.89 4.9a1 1 0 0 0 1.41-1.41L13.41 12l4.9-4.89a1 1 0 0 0-.01-1.4z');
    path.setAttribute('fill', 'currentColor');
    svg.appendChild(path);
    closeBtn.appendChild(svg);
    card.appendChild(closeBtn);

    // Header image links to product
    var linkImg = document.createElement('a');
    linkImg.className = 'wdw-header-link';
    linkImg.href = conf.CTA_HREF || '#';
    linkImg.setAttribute('aria-label', conf.CTA_TEXT || 'Join DCL Magazine');
    var img = document.createElement('img');
    img.className = 'wdw-header-img';
    img.src = conf.IMG || '';
    img.alt = 'DCL Magazine &ndash; Disney Cruise Line magazine';
    linkImg.appendChild(img);
    card.appendChild(linkImg);

    var content = document.createElement('div');
    content.className = 'wdw-content';

    // Pick a random promo line for this load
    var lines = Array.isArray(conf.PROMO_LINES) ? conf.PROMO_LINES : [];
    var promo = lines.length
      ? lines[Math.floor(Math.random() * lines.length)]
      : 'Set sail with the first-ever print magazine dedicated to Disney Cruise Line &ndash; join DCL Magazine today.';

    var p1 = document.createElement('p');
    p1.id = 'wdwHeading';
    p1.className = 'wdw-text';
    p1.textContent = promo;
    content.appendChild(p1);

    var cta = document.createElement('a');
    cta.className = 'wdw-cta';
    cta.href = conf.CTA_HREF || '#';
    cta.textContent = conf.CTA_TEXT || 'Join DCL Magazine Today';
    content.appendChild(cta);

    card.appendChild(content);
    modal.appendChild(card);
    document.body.appendChild(frag);

    // --- Wire interactions ---
    function reallyRemove(){
      try{ backdrop && backdrop.remove(); }catch(e){}
      try{ modal && modal.remove(); }catch(e){}
      document.body.classList.remove(BODY_OPEN_CLASS);
      lockScroll(false);
    }

    function closeAndRemove(setTs){
      backdrop && backdrop.classList.remove('wdw-visible');
      card && card.classList.remove('wdw-in');

      var done = false;
      function tidy(){
        if(done) return; done = true;
        backdrop && backdrop.removeEventListener('transitionend', tidy);
        reallyRemove();
        if (setTs) setSuppress();
        if (SHOW_FLOAT){
          var pill = document.getElementById('wdwFloatBtn');
          if (pill) pill.style.display = 'block';
        }
        document.removeEventListener('keydown', escHandler);
      }
      backdrop && backdrop.addEventListener('transitionend', tidy);
      setTimeout(tidy, 350);
    }

    function escHandler(e){
      if(e.key==='Escape'){ closeAndRemove(true); }
    }

    closeBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e){ e.preventDefault(); closeAndRemove(true); });
    backdrop.addEventListener('click', function(){ closeAndRemove(true); });
    document.addEventListener('keydown', escHandler);

    // Show sequence
    requestAnimationFrame(function(){
      document.body.classList.add(BODY_OPEN_CLASS);
      lockScroll(true);
      backdrop.classList.add('wdw-visible');
      requestAnimationFrame(function(){ card.classList.add('wdw-in'); try{ card.focus(); }catch(e){} });
    });

    return { backdrop: backdrop, modal: modal, card: card, closeAndRemove: closeAndRemove };
  }

  // Reopen pill (render once)
  function ensureFloatBtn(){
    if (!SHOW_FLOAT) return null;

    var pill = document.getElementById('wdwFloatBtn');
    if (!pill){
      pill = document.createElement('div');
      pill.id = 'wdwFloatBtn';
      pill.className = 'wdw-float-btn';
      pill.style.display = 'none';

      var s1 = document.createElement('span'); s1.textContent = conf.FLOAT_L1 || '';
      var s2 = document.createElement('span'); s2.textContent = conf.FLOAT_L2 || '';
      pill.appendChild(s1); pill.appendChild(s2);

      document.body.appendChild(pill);
    }

    function openFromPill(e){
      e.preventDefault(); e.stopPropagation();
      pill.style.display = 'none';
      buildPopup();
    }
    pill.addEventListener('click', openFromPill);
    pill.addEventListener('touchstart', openFromPill, {passive:false});

    pill.setAttribute('role','button');
    pill.setAttribute('tabindex','0');
    pill.setAttribute('aria-label','Reopen DCL Magazine offer');
    pill.addEventListener('keydown', function(e){
      if(e.key === 'Enter' || e.key === ' '){
        e.preventDefault(); openFromPill(e);
      }
    });

    return pill;
  }

  // Boot logic
  var pill = ensureFloatBtn();

  if (!shouldSuppress()){
    var start = function(){ buildPopup(); };
    if(document.readyState === 'loading'){
      document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function(){ setTimeout(start, SHOW_DELAY_MS); });
    } else {
      setTimeout(start, SHOW_DELAY_MS);
    }
  } else if (pill) {
    pill.style.display = 'block';
  }

  // Safety on navigation
  window.addEventListener('pagehide', function(){
    var b = document.getElementById('wdwBackdrop');
    var m = document.getElementById('wdwModal');
    if(b) try{ b.remove(); }catch(e){}
    if(m) try{ m.remove(); }catch(e){}
    document.body.classList.remove(BODY_OPEN_CLASS);
    lockScroll(false);
  });
})();

(function(){
  if (window._wdw_membership_init) return;
  window._wdw_membership_init = true;

  function qs(s,el){return (el||document).querySelector(s);}
  function qsa(s,el){return [].slice.call((el||document).querySelectorAll(s));}

  function wdwToastInline(message, type){
    const slot = qs('.wdw-toast-slot');
    if(!slot) return;
    slot.innerHTML = '';
    const el = document.createElement('div');
    el.className = 'wdw-toast-inline' + (type ? (' '+type) : ' success');
    el.textContent = message || '';
    slot.appendChild(el);
    requestAnimationFrame(()=> el.classList.add('show'));
    setTimeout(()=> {
      el.classList.remove('show');
      setTimeout(()=> { if (el.parentNode) el.parentNode.removeChild(el); }, 180);
    }, 2200);
  }

  function showLoader(text){
    const L = qs('.wdw-loader');
    if(!L) return;
    const t = L.querySelector('.wdw-loader-text');
    if(t && text) t.textContent = text;
    L.style.display = 'flex';
  }
  function hideLoader(){
    const L = qs('.wdw-loader');
    if(!L) return;
    L.style.display = 'none';
  }

  let _scrollY = 0;
  function lockScroll(){
    _scrollY = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop || 0;
    document.documentElement.classList.add('wdw-scroll-lock','wdw-lock');
    document.body.classList.add('wdw-lock');
    document.body.style.top = '-' + _scrollY + 'px';
  }
  function unlockScroll(){
    document.documentElement.classList.remove('wdw-scroll-lock','wdw-lock');
    document.body.classList.remove('wdw-lock');
    document.body.style.top = '';
    window.scrollTo(0, _scrollY);
  }

  function setStep(n){
    showLoader('Loading&hellip;');
    setTimeout(()=>{
      qsa('.wdw-wiz-step').forEach((el,i)=>el.classList.toggle('active',(i+1)===n));
      qsa('[data-step]').forEach(el=>{
        el.style.display = (Number(el.getAttribute('data-step'))===n)?'block':'none';
      });
      if(n===1) renderStep1();
      if(n===2) renderStep2();
      if(n===3) renderStep3();
      if(n===4) renderStep4();
      hideLoader();
    }, 120);
  }

  function openWizard(){
    const overlay = qs('.wdw-wiz-overlay');
    const modal   = qs('.wdw-wiz-modal');
    if (!overlay || !modal) {
      console.warn('[WDW Membership Wizard] Markup not found. Ensure [wdw_membership_wizard] shortcode is on this page.');
      return;
    }
    const title = qs('.wdw-wiz-title', modal);
    if(title){
      title.textContent = 'Build Your Membership';
    }
    const sub = qs('.wdw-wiz-sub', modal);
    if(sub){
      sub.innerHTML = 'Pick your print membership, choose duration, add digital, then optionally add a <strong>free issue</strong> (shipping still applies).';
    }
    overlay.style.display = 'block';
    modal.style.display   = 'block';
    lockScroll();
    setStep(1);
  }

  function closeWizard(){
    const overlay = qs('.wdw-wiz-overlay');
    const modal   = qs('.wdw-wiz-modal');
    if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none';
    if (modal)   modal.style.display   = 'none';
    unlockScroll();
  }

  function openDescModal(title, productId){
    const o = qs('.wdw-desc-overlay'),
          m = qs('.wdw-desc-modal');
    if(!o || !m) return;
    qs('.wdw-desc-title', m).textContent = title || 'Details';
    qs('.wdw-desc-body', m).innerHTML = '<p>Loading&hellip;</p>';
    o.style.display='block';
    m.style.display='block';

    const fd = new FormData();
    fd.append('action','wdw_membership_get_desc');
    fd.append('nonce', WDW_MEMBERSHIP.nonce);
    fd.append('product_id', productId);

    fetch(WDW_MEMBERSHIP.ajax, {
      method:'POST',
      body:fd,
      credentials:'same-origin'
    }).then(r=>r.json()).then(j=>{
      if(j && j.success){
        qs('.wdw-desc-body', m).innerHTML = '<div class="content">'+(j.data.html||'')+'</div>';
      } else {
        qs('.wdw-desc-body', m).innerHTML = '<p>Sorry, description unavailable.</p>';
      }
    }).catch(()=>{
      qs('.wdw-desc-body', m).innerHTML = '<p>Network error.</p>';
    });
  }

  function closeDescModal(){
    const o = qs('.wdw-desc-overlay'),
          m = qs('.wdw-desc-modal');
    if(o) o.style.display='none';
    if(m) m.style.display='none';
  }

  // ========== GLOBAL CLICK HANDLING ==========
  document.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
    const t = e.target;

    // Main open button (shortcode button)
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-open]')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      openWizard();
      return;
    }

    // Text link trigger
    const linkTrigger = t.closest('[data-wdw-open-link]');
    if (linkTrigger) {
      e.preventDefault();
      openWizard();
      return;
    }

    // Main wizard close button
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-close]')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      closeWizard();
      return;
    }

    // CLICK OFF (overlay) TO CLOSE MAIN WIZARD
    if (t.matches('.wdw-wiz-overlay')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      closeWizard();
      return;
    }

    // Description modal close & click-off
    if (t.matches('.wdw-desc-overlay') || t.matches('[data-wdw-desc-close]')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      closeDescModal();
      return;
    }
  });

  // Tabs &mdash; step switching
  document.addEventListener('click', (e)=>{
    const tab = e.target.closest('.wdw-wiz-step');
    if(!tab) return;
    const idx = Array.from(qsa('.wdw-wiz-step')).indexOf(tab);
    if(idx>=0){
      setStep(idx+1);
    }
  });

  // Learn more buttons
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    const btn = e.target.closest('[data-learn]');
    if(!btn) return;
    e.preventDefault();
    e.stopPropagation();
    openDescModal(btn.getAttribute('data-learn-title')||'Details', btn.getAttribute('data-learn'));
  });

  // ====== AUTO-OPEN VIA URL (HASH OR ?open=wdw-membership) ======
  function shouldAutoOpen(){
    const hash = (window.location.hash||'').toLowerCase();
    if(hash === '#wdw-membership') return true;
    const qsParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    if((qsParams.get('open')||'').toLowerCase() === 'wdw-membership') return true;
    return false;
  }

  function autoOpenFromUrlIfNeeded(){
    if (!shouldAutoOpen()) return;

    let tries = 0;
    const maxTries = 30;
    function attempt(){
      const overlay = qs('.wdw-wiz-overlay');
      const modal   = qs('.wdw-wiz-modal');
      if (overlay && modal) {
        openWizard();
      } else if (++tries < maxTries) {
        setTimeout(attempt, 150);
      } else {
        console.warn('[WDW Membership Wizard] Auto-open requested via URL, but markup not found after waiting.');
      }
    }
    attempt();
  }

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', autoOpenFromUrlIfNeeded);
  } else {
    autoOpenFromUrlIfNeeded();
  }

  // ===== State
  const state = {
    choice:null,
    plan:null,
    addDigital:false,
    freeIssue:{wdw:false, dlr:false}
  };

  // ===== Step 1 &mdash; CHOOSE (WDW / DLR / DCL / FULL BUNDLE LAST)
  function renderStep1(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step1');
    if(!wrap) return;
    const M = (window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP || {});
    const I = M.images || {};
    const T = M.titles || {};
    const cfg = M.cfg || {};

    function row(key, img, title, learnTitle, learnPid, note){
      const selected = (state.choice === key) ? ' style="outline:2px solid #111"' : '';
      return (
        '<div class="wdw-row" data-choice="'+key+'"' + selected + '>' +
          '<div class="left">' +
            (img ? ('<img src="'+img+'" alt="'+title+'">') : '') +
            '<div>' +
              '<div class="title">'+title+'</div>' +
              (note ? '<div class="wdw-note" style="margin-top:4px">'+note+'</div>' : '') +
              (learnPid ? '<div class="wdw-learn" style="margin-top:8px">' +
                '<button type="button" class="wdw-btn secondary"' +
                  ' data-learn="'+learnPid+'"' +
                  ' data-learn-title="'+(learnTitle || title)+'">Learn more</button>' +
              '</div>' : '' ) +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="right">' +
            '<button class="wdw-btn addnow" data-choose="'+key+'">Select</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>'
      );
    }

    const rows = [];

    // WDW
    rows.push(
      row(
        'wdw',
        I.wdw,
        'WDW Magazine',
        T.wdw,
        cfg.wdw ? cfg.wdw.monthly : 0,
        'Monthly &bull; Quarterly &bull; Annual'
      )
    );

    // DLR
    rows.push(
      row(
        'dlr',
        I.dlr,
        'DLR Magazine',
        T.dlr,
        cfg.dlr ? cfg.dlr.quarterly : 0,
        'Quarterly &bull; Annual'
      )
    );

    // DCL
    rows.push(
      row(
        'dcl',
        I.dcl || I.combo || '',
        'DCL Magazine',
        T.dcl || 'DCL Magazine',
        cfg.dcl ? (cfg.dcl.semi_annual || cfg.dcl.annual || 0) : 0,
        'Semi-Annual &bull; Annual'
      )
    );

    // FULL BUNDLE
    rows.push(
      row(
        'both',
        I.combo || I.wdw || '',
        'Full Bundle (WDW + DLR + DCL)',
        'All Publications',
        0,
        'Best-value bundle of all magazines'
      )
    );

    wrap.innerHTML = rows.join('');

    wrap.onclick = (ev)=>{
      const chooseBtn = ev.target.closest('[data-choose]');
      if(!chooseBtn) return;
      const key = chooseBtn.getAttribute('data-choose');
      state.choice = key;
      if(state.choice!=='wdw' && state.plan==='monthly'){
        state.plan = null;
      }
      state.freeIssue.wdw = false;
      state.freeIssue.dlr = false;

      const labelMap = {
        wdw: 'WDW',
        dlr: 'DLR',
        dcl: 'DCL',
        both: 'Full Bundle'
      };
      wdwToastInline('Selected ' + (labelMap[key] || key.toUpperCase()), 'success');
      setTimeout(()=> setStep(2), 350);
    };
  }

  // ===== Step 2 &mdash; DURATION
  function renderStep2(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step2');
    if(!wrap) return;
    const M = (window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP||{});
    const I = M.images || {};
    const P = M.prices || {};

    if(!state.choice){
      wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="wdw-note">Choose a membership first.</div>';
      return;
    }

    const caps = {
      monthly: 'Monthly',
      quarterly: 'Quarterly',
      semi_annual: 'Semi-Annual',
      annual: 'Annual'
    };
    const baseTerms = {
      monthly: 'Renews every month. Cancel anytime.',
      quarterly: 'Renews every 3 months. Cancel anytime.',
      semi_annual: 'Charges every 6 months. Cancel anytime.',
      annual: 'Renews every 12 months. Best for savings.'
    };

    let headImg, headTitle;
    if (state.choice === 'wdw'){
      headImg = I.wdw;
      headTitle = 'WDW Magazine';
    } else if (state.choice === 'dlr'){
      headImg = I.dlr;
      headTitle = 'DLR Magazine';
    } else if (state.choice === 'dcl'){
      headImg = I.dcl || I.combo;
      headTitle = 'DCL Magazine';
    } else {
      headImg = I.combo;
      headTitle = 'Full Bundle (WDW + DLR + DCL)';
    }

    let options;
    if (state.choice === 'wdw'){
      options = ['monthly','quarterly','annual'];
    } else if (state.choice === 'dlr'){
      options = ['quarterly','annual'];
    } else if (state.choice === 'dcl'){
      options = ['semi_annual','annual'];
    } else {
      options = ['quarterly','annual'];
    }

    let html = '';
    options.forEach(function(k){
      let priceStr = '';
      if (state.choice === 'wdw') {
        priceStr = (P.wdw && P.wdw[k]) ? P.wdw[k] : '';
      } else if (state.choice === 'dlr') {
        priceStr = (P.dlr && P.dlr[k]) ? P.dlr[k] : '';
      } else if (state.choice === 'dcl') {
        priceStr = (P.dcl && P.dcl[k]) ? P.dcl[k] : '';
      } else {
        const pW = (P.wdw && P.wdw[k]) ? P.wdw[k] : '';
        const pD = (P.dlr && P.dlr[k]) ? P.dlr[k] : '';
        priceStr = (pW || pD) ? (pW + ' + ' + pD) : '';
      }

      const badge = (k==='annual') ? '<span class="wdw-badge-in" style="margin-left:8px">Best Value</span>' : '';
      const saveBoth = (state.choice==='both') ? '<span class="wdw-save" style="margin-left:8px">10% off WDW & DLR</span>' : '';
      let termCopy = baseTerms[k] || '';

      if (k === 'semi_annual') {
        termCopy = 'Charges every 6 months. Cancel anytime.';
      }

      if (k === 'annual') {
        if (state.choice === 'dcl') {
          termCopy = 'Renews every 12 months. Includes DCL calendar preorders.';
        } else if (state.choice === 'wdw' || state.choice === 'dlr' || state.choice === 'both') {
          termCopy = 'Renews every 12 months. Includes DCL Magazine annual (with calendar preorders).';
        }
      }

      html += (
        '<div class="wdw-row" data-plan="'+k+'">' +
          '<div class="left">' +
            (headImg ? '<img src="'+headImg+'" alt="'+headTitle+'">' : '') +
            '<div>' +
              '<div class="title">'+headTitle+' &mdash; '+(caps[k] || k)+badge+saveBoth+'</div>' +
              (priceStr ? '<div class="wdw-note" style="margin-top:4px">'+priceStr+'</div>' : '') +
              '<div class="wdw-plan-terms" style="margin-top:6px">'+termCopy+'</div>' +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="right">' +
            '<button class="wdw-btn addnow" data-choose-plan="'+k+'">Select</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>'
      );
    });

    if(state.choice==='both'){
      html += '<div class="wdw-note" style="margin:6px 2px 0">Bundle includes WDW & DLR (10% off both print). Annual bundles also include <strong>DCL Magazine annual</strong> with calendar preorders.</div>';
    } else if (state.choice === 'wdw' || state.choice === 'dlr') {
      html += '<div class="wdw-note" style="margin:6px 2px 0">Annual print memberships include <strong>DCL Magazine annual</strong> with calendar preorders.</div>';
    }

    wrap.innerHTML = html;

    wrap.onclick = (ev)=>{
      const btn = ev.target.closest('[data-choose-plan]');
      if(!btn) return;
      const plan = btn.getAttribute('data-choose-plan');
      state.plan = plan;
      const label = caps[plan] || plan;
      wdwToastInline('Selected ' + label, 'success');
      setTimeout(()=> setStep(3), 350);
    };
  }

  // ===== Step 3 &mdash; Digital (15% off)
  function renderStep3(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step3');
    if(!wrap) return;
    const M = (window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP||{});
    const I = M.images||{};
    const T = M.titles||{};
    const cfg = M.cfg ||{};

    if(!state.choice || !state.plan){
      wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="wdw-note">Complete the previous steps first.</div>';
      return;
    }

    const planLabelMap = {
      monthly: 'Monthly',
      quarterly: 'Quarterly',
      semi_annual: 'Semi-Annual',
      annual: 'Annual'
    };
    const planLabel = planLabelMap[state.plan] || '';

    wrap.innerHTML = '' +
      '<div class="wdw-row">' +
        '<div class="left">' +
          (I.digital?'<img src="'+I.digital+'" alt="All-Access Digital Membership">':'') +
          '<div>' +
            '<div class="title">Add All-Access Digital ('+planLabel+') &mdash; 15% Off</div>' +
            '<div class="wdw-learn" style="margin-top:8px">' +
              '<button type="button" class="wdw-btn secondary" data-learn="'+(cfg.digital.monthly)+'" data-learn-title="'+(T.digital||'All-Access Digital')+'">Learn more</button>' +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="right">' +
          '<button class="wdw-btn addnow" id="wdw-add-digital-btn">Add Now</button>' +
          '<button class="wdw-btn ghost" id="wdw-skip-digital-btn">Skip</button>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>';

    const addBtn  = qs('#wdw-add-digital-btn', wrap);
    const skipBtn = qs('#wdw-skip-digital-btn', wrap);

    if (addBtn){
      addBtn.onclick = ()=>{
        state.addDigital = true;
        wdwToastInline('Added Digital (15% off)', 'success');
        setTimeout(()=> setStep(4), 350);
      };
    }
    if (skipBtn){
      skipBtn.onclick = ()=>{
        state.addDigital = false;
        wdwToastInline('Skipped Digital', 'info');
        setTimeout(()=> setStep(4), 350);
      };
    }
  }

  // ===== Step 4 &mdash; Free Issue add-on (WDW/DLR only; $0 line, shipping applies)
  function renderStep4(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step4');
    if(!wrap) return;
    const M = (window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP||{});
    const I = M.images||{};
    const T = M.titles||{};
    const cfg = M.cfg||{};
    const pidW = cfg.free_issue ? cfg.free_issue.wdw : 0;
    const pidD = cfg.free_issue ? cfg.free_issue.dlr : 0;

    if(!state.choice || !state.plan){
      wrap.innerHTML = '<div class="wdw-note">Complete the previous steps first.</div>';
      return;
    }

    const allowWDW = (state.choice === 'wdw' || state.choice === 'both');
    const allowDLR = (state.choice === 'dlr' || state.choice === 'both');

    let html = '';
    html += '<div class="wdw-note" style="margin:2px 2px 10px;">Add a free issue to your order. <strong>You&rsquo;ll still pay shipping &amp; handling.</strong></div>';

    if(allowWDW){
      html += '' +
        '<div class="wdw-row">' +
          '<div class="left">' +
            (I.free_wdw?'<img src="'+I.free_wdw+'" alt="Free WDW Issue">':'') +
            '<div>' +
              '<div class="title">Add FREE WDW Issue</div>' +
              '<div class="wdw-note" style="margin-top:4px">Product: '+(T.free_wdw || 'WDW Free Issue')+' &bull; Price: $0 (shipping still applies)</div>' +
              (pidW?('<div class="wdw-learn" style="margin-top:8px"><button type="button" class="wdw-btn secondary" data-learn="'+pidW+'" data-learn-title="'+(T.free_wdw||'Free WDW Issue')+'">Learn more</button></div>'):'') +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="right">' +
            '<button class="wdw-btn addnow" data-toggle-free="wdw">'+(state.freeIssue.wdw ? 'Added' : 'Add')+'</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    }

    if(allowDLR){
      html += '' +
        '<div class="wdw-row">' +
          '<div class="left">' +
            (I.free_dlr?'<img src="'+I.free_dlr+'" alt="Free DLR Issue">':'') +
            '<div>' +
              '<div class="title">Add FREE DLR Issue</div>' +
              '<div class="wdw-note" style="margin-top:4px">Product: '+(T.free_dlr || 'DLR Free Issue')+' &bull; Price: $0 (shipping still applies)</div>' +
              (pidD?('<div class="wdw-learn" style="margin-top:8px"><button type="button" class="wdw-btn secondary" data-learn="'+pidD+'" data-learn-title="'+(T.free_dlr||'Free DLR Issue')+'">Learn more</button></div>'):'') +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="right">' +
            '<button class="wdw-btn addnow" data-toggle-free="dlr">'+(state.freeIssue.dlr ? 'Added' : 'Add')+'</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    }

    html += '<div class="wdw-wiz-foot" style="justify-content:flex-end;padding:0;margin-top:6px;">' +
              '<button class="wdw-btn addnow" id="wdw-finish-btn">Continue to Checkout</button>' +
            '</div>';

    wrap.innerHTML = html;

    wrap.onclick = (ev)=>{
      const tgl = ev.target.closest('[data-toggle-free]');
      if(tgl){
        const which = tgl.getAttribute('data-toggle-free');
        if(which === 'wdw'){
          state.freeIssue.wdw = !state.freeIssue.wdw;
          wdwToastInline(state.freeIssue.wdw ? 'Added FREE WDW issue' : 'Removed FREE WDW issue', 'info');
        }
        if(which === 'dlr'){
          state.freeIssue.dlr = !state.freeIssue.dlr;
          wdwToastInline(state.freeIssue.dlr ? 'Added FREE DLR issue' : 'Removed FREE DLR issue', 'info');
        }
        renderStep4();
        return;
      }

      const fin = ev.target.closest('#wdw-finish-btn');
      if(fin){
        const submit = qs('[data-submit-wiz]');
        if(submit){
          submit.click();
        }
      }
    };
  }

  // ===== Submit
  document.addEventListener('click',(e)=>{
    const t=e.target;
    if(!t.matches('[data-submit-wiz]')) return;
    e.preventDefault();

    if(!state.choice || !state.plan){
      alert('Please complete your selections.');
      return;
    }

    const cfg = window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP.cfg,
          items=[];

    function addBase(pid, override){
      const o = override || {};
      items.push(Object.assign({product_id:pid, quantity:1}, o));
    }

    // Print membership(s)
    if(state.choice==='wdw'){
      addBase(cfg.wdw[state.plan]);
    } else if(state.choice==='dlr'){
      addBase(cfg.dlr[state.plan]);
    } else if(state.choice==='dcl'){
      addBase(cfg.dcl[state.plan]);
    } else if(state.choice==='both'){
      const override10 = { override_mode:'PERCENT_OFF', override_value:10 };
      addBase(cfg.wdw[state.plan], override10);
      addBase(cfg.dlr[state.plan], override10);
    }

    // If user chose any ANNUAL print plan (WDW / DLR / BUNDLE),
    // also include DCL Annual as part of the benefit, unless they're
    // already on the DCL standalone plan.
    if (state.plan === 'annual' && cfg.dcl && cfg.dcl.annual && state.choice !== 'dcl'){
      addBase(cfg.dcl.annual);
    }

    // Digital (align semi_annual -> annual for digital, if needed)
    if(state.addDigital){
      const digitalKey = (state.plan === 'semi_annual') ? 'annual' : state.plan;
      const digPid = cfg.digital[digitalKey];
      if(digPid){
        items.push({
          product_id:digPid,
          quantity:1,
          override_mode:'PERCENT_OFF',
          override_value:15
        });
      }
    }

    // Free issue(s)
    if(cfg.free_issue){
      if(state.freeIssue.wdw && cfg.free_issue.wdw){
        items.push({
          product_id:cfg.free_issue.wdw,
          quantity:1,
          override_mode:'SET_PRICE',
          override_value:0.00,
          lock_price:true,
          note:'Free issue'
        });
      }
      if(state.freeIssue.dlr && cfg.free_issue.dlr){
        items.push({
          product_id:cfg.free_issue.dlr,
          quantity:1,
          override_mode:'SET_PRICE',
          override_value:0.00,
          lock_price:true,
          note:'Free issue'
        });
      }
    }

    const fd = new FormData();
    fd.append('action','wdw_membership_add_to_cart');
    fd.append('nonce', window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP.nonce);
    fd.append('payload', JSON.stringify({items}));

    t.disabled=true;
    t.textContent='Adding...';
    showLoader('Adding to cart&hellip;');

    fetch(window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP.ajax,{
      method:'POST',
      body:fd,
      credentials:'same-origin'
    })
    .then(r=>r.json())
    .then(j=>{
      if(!j.success){
        t.disabled=false;
        t.textContent='Add to Cart';
        hideLoader();
        wdwToastInline((j.data&&j.data.message) ? j.data.message : 'Unable to add to cart.', 'error');
        return;
      }
      showLoader('Redirecting to checkout&hellip;');
      setTimeout(()=> {
        window.location = window.WDW_MEMBERSHIP.redirect || '/checkout-2/';
      }, 450);
    })
    .catch(()=>{
      t.disabled=false;
      t.textContent='Add to Cart';
      hideLoader();
      wdwToastInline('Network error. Please try again.', 'error');
    });
  });

  window.WDW_OPEN_MEMBERSHIP = openWizard;
})();

  window._wdw_pub_wizard_init = true;

  const DATA = window.WDW_PUBLICATION || {};
  const PUBS = DATA.pubs || {};
  const FREE = DATA.freeIssues || [];
  const ADDON_DISC = DATA.addonsDisc || 10;

  // Ensure overlays & modals are at the very end of <body> so they sit above side carts/popups
  (function moveWizardToBodyEnd(){
    if (!document.body) return;
    const selectors = [
      '.wdw-pub-overlay',
      '.wdw-pub-modal',
      '.wdw-pub-desc-overlay',
      '.wdw-pub-desc-modal'
    ];
    selectors.forEach(sel => {
      const el = document.querySelector(sel);
      if (el) {
        // appending again moves it to the end of <body>
        document.body.appendChild(el);
      }
    });
  })();

  function qs(sel, root){ return (root||document).querySelector(sel); }
  function qsa(sel, root){ return Array.prototype.slice.call((root||document).querySelectorAll(sel)); }

  /* Toasts */
  function toast(message, type) {
    const slot = qs('.wdw-pub-toast-slot');
    if (!slot) return;
    slot.innerHTML = '';
    const div = document.createElement('div');
    div.className = 'wdw-pub-toast' + (type ? (' ' + type) : '');
    div.textContent = message || '';
    slot.appendChild(div);
    requestAnimationFrame(()=> div.classList.add('show'));
    setTimeout(()=>{
      div.classList.remove('show');
      setTimeout(()=>{ if (div.parentNode) div.parentNode.removeChild(div); }, 180);
    }, 2600);
  }

  /* Loader */
  function showLoader(text){
    const L = qs('.wdw-pub-loader');
    if (!L) return;
    const t = qs('.wdw-pub-loader-text', L);
    if (t && text) t.textContent = text;
    L.style.display = 'flex';
  }
  function hideLoader(){
    const L = qs('.wdw-pub-loader');
    if (!L) return;
    L.style.display = 'none';
  }

  /* Scroll lock */
  let scrollY = 0;
  function lockScroll(){
    scrollY = window.scrollY || document.documentElement.scrollTop || 0;
    document.documentElement.classList.add('wdw-pub-lock');
    document.body.classList.add('wdw-pub-lock');
    document.body.style.top = '-' + scrollY + 'px';
  }
  function unlockScroll(){
    document.documentElement.classList.remove('wdw-pub-lock');
    document.body.classList.remove('wdw-pub-lock');
    document.body.style.top = '';
    window.scrollTo(0, scrollY);
  }

  /* State */
  const state = {
    primaryKey: null,
    plan: null,
    addOns: [],
    freeIssues: [],
    orderPayload: null
  };

  let currentDescFreeId = null;
  let currentStep = 1;

  function resetState(){
    state.plan = null;
    state.addOns = [];
    state.freeIssues = [];
    state.orderPayload = null;
  }

  /* Modal open / close */
  function openWizard(initialStep){
    const overlay = qs('.wdw-pub-overlay');
    const modal   = qs('.wdw-pub-modal');
    if (!overlay || !modal) return;
    overlay.style.display = 'block';
    modal.style.display   = 'flex'; // flex so body can scroll between header & footer
    lockScroll();
    setStep(initialStep || 1);
  }

  function closeWizard(){
    const overlay = qs('.wdw-pub-overlay');
    const modal   = qs('.wdw-pub-modal');
    if (overlay) overlay.style.display = 'none';
    if (modal)   modal.style.display   = 'none';
    unlockScroll();
  }

  function updateDescSelectButton(){
    const btn = qs('[data-wdw-pub-desc-select]');
    if (!btn) return;
    if (!currentDescFreeId) {
      btn.style.display = 'none';
      return;
    }
    btn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
    const selected = state.freeIssues.indexOf(currentDescFreeId) >= 0;
    btn.textContent = selected ? 'Remove This Free Issue' : 'Select This Free Issue';
  }

  function openDescModal(title, productId, opts){
    const o = qs('.wdw-pub-desc-overlay');
    const m = qs('.wdw-pub-desc-modal');
    if (!o || !m) return;

    currentDescFreeId = (opts && typeof opts.freeId !== 'undefined')
      ? parseInt(opts.freeId, 10)
      : null;
    updateDescSelectButton();

    qs('.wdw-pub-desc-title', m).textContent = title || 'Details';
    const body = qs('.wdw-pub-desc-body', m);
    if (body) body.innerHTML = '<p>Loading details&hellip;</p>';
    o.style.display = 'block';
    m.style.display = 'block';

    const fd = new FormData();
    fd.append('action', 'wdw_publication_get_desc');
    fd.append('nonce', DATA.nonce || '');
    fd.append('product_id', String(productId || ''));

    fetch(DATA.ajax, {
      method:'POST',
      body:fd,
      credentials:'same-origin'
    }).then(r=>r.json()).then(j=>{
      if (!body) return;
      if (!j || !j.success) {
        body.innerHTML = '<p>Sorry, details are unavailable.</p>';
        return;
      }
      const html = j.data && j.data.html ? j.data.html : '';
      const gallery = j.data && j.data.gallery ? j.data.gallery : '';
      body.innerHTML =
        (gallery ? '<div class="wdw-pub-desc-gallery">'+gallery+'</div>' : '') +
        '<div class="wdw-pub-desc-content">'+html+'</div>';
    }).catch(()=>{
      if (body) body.innerHTML = '<p>Network error. Please try again.</p>';
    });
  }

  function closeDescModal(){
    const o = qs('.wdw-pub-desc-overlay');
    const m = qs('.wdw-pub-desc-modal');
    if (o) o.style.display = 'none';
    if (m) m.style.display = 'none';
    currentDescFreeId = null;
    updateDescSelectButton();
  }

  /* Steps */
  const PLAN_LABELS = {
    monthly: 'Monthly',
    quarterly: 'Quarterly',
    semi_annual: 'Semi-Annual',
    annual: 'Annual'
  };

  function setStep(n){
    currentStep = n;
    const steps = qsa('.wdw-pub-step');
    steps.forEach((el, idx)=>{
      const isActive = (idx+1) === n;
      el.classList.toggle('active', isActive);
      el.setAttribute('aria-selected', isActive ? 'true' : 'false');
    });

    const panes = qsa('.wdw-pub-step-pane');
    panes.forEach((p,idx)=>{
      p.classList.toggle('active', (idx+1) === n);
    });

    // Show Next button on steps 1&ndash;4 only
    const nextBtn = qs('[data-wdw-pub-next]');
    if (nextBtn) {
      nextBtn.style.display = (n < 5 ? '' : 'none');
    }

    showLoader('Sprinkling pixie dust&hellip;');
    setTimeout(()=>{
      if (n===1) renderStep1();
      if (n===2) renderStep2();
      if (n===3) renderStep3();
      if (n===4) renderStep4();
      if (n===5) renderStep5();
      hideLoader();
    }, 120);
  }

  function getPlanProductId(pubKey, planKey){
    const d = PUBS[pubKey];
    if (!d) return null;
    const m = d.products || {};
    if (m[planKey]) return m[planKey];
    const order = ['annual','quarterly','monthly','semi_annual'];
    for (let i=0;i<order.length;i++){
      const k = order[i];
      if (m[k]) return m[k];
    }
    return null;
  }

  function renderStep1(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step1');
    if (!wrap) return;

    const keys = Object.keys(PUBS);
    let html = '';
    keys.forEach(k=>{
      const d = PUBS[k];
      const img = d.image || '';
      const selected = (state.primaryKey === k) ? ' main-selected' : '';
      const caps = d.label || k.toUpperCase();
      const tagline = d.tagline || '';
      html +=
        '<div class="wdw-pub-row'+selected+'" data-primary-choice="'+k+'">' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-row-left">' +
            (img ? '<img src="'+img+'" alt="'+caps+'">' : '') +
            '<div class="wdw-pub-row-titles">' +
              '<div class="wdw-pub-row-title-line">'+caps+'</div>' +
              (tagline ? '<div class="wdw-pub-row-subline">'+tagline+'</div>' : '') +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-row-right">' +
            '<button class="wdw-pub-btn" data-primary-btn="'+k+'">Choose</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    });

    wrap.innerHTML = html;

    wrap.onclick = function(ev){
      const row = ev.target.closest('[data-primary-choice]');
      const btn = ev.target.closest('[data-primary-btn]');
      const target = btn || row;
      if (!target) return;
      const key = target.getAttribute(btn ? 'data-primary-btn' : 'data-primary-choice');
      if (!key) return;
      state.primaryKey = key;
      resetState();
      toast('Great choice! Now pick your renewal.', 'info');
      setTimeout(()=> setStep(2), 280);
    };
  }

  function renderStep2(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step2');
    if (!wrap) return;

    if (!state.primaryKey || !PUBS[state.primaryKey]) {
      wrap.innerHTML = '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">Choose a primary publication first.</p>';
      return;
    }

    const pub = PUBS[state.primaryKey];
    const img = pub.image || '';
    const prods = pub.products || {};
    const keys = Object.keys(prods);
    const prices = pub.prices || {};

    let html = '';
    keys.forEach(plan=>{
      const price = prices[plan] || '';
      const label = PLAN_LABELS[plan] || plan;
      const selected = (state.plan === plan) ? ' main-selected' : '';
      const isAnnual = (plan === 'annual');
      const meta =
        plan==='monthly'   ? 'Renews every month. Cancel anytime.' :
        plan==='quarterly' ? 'Renews every 3 months. Cancel anytime.' :
        plan==='semi_annual' ? 'Charges every 6 months. Cancel anytime.' :
        'Renews every 12 months. Best value.';

      html +=
        '<div class="wdw-pub-row'+selected+'" data-plan-choice="'+plan+'">' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-row-left">' +
            (img ? '<img src="'+img+'" alt="'+pub.label+'">' : '') +
            '<div class="wdw-pub-row-titles">' +
              '<div class="wdw-pub-row-title-line">'+pub.label+' &mdash; '+label+(isAnnual ? ' <span style="font-weight:600;color:#16a34a;">(Best for savings)</span>' : '')+'</div>' +
              (price ? '<div class="wdw-pub-row-subline">'+price+'</div>' : '') +
              '<div class="wdw-pub-row-meta">'+meta+'</div>' +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-row-right">' +
            (isAnnual?'<span class="wdw-pub-pill best">BEST VALUE</span>':'<span class="wdw-pub-pill">Flexible</span>') +
            '<button class="wdw-pub-btn" data-plan-btn="'+plan+'">Choose</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    });

    wrap.innerHTML = html;

    wrap.onclick = function(ev){
      const row = ev.target.closest('[data-plan-choice]');
      const btn = ev.target.closest('[data-plan-btn]');
      const target = btn || row;
      if (!target) return;
      const plan = target.getAttribute(btn ? 'data-plan-btn' : 'data-plan-choice');
      if (!plan) return;
      state.plan = plan;
      toast('Renewal set to '+(PLAN_LABELS[plan] || plan)+'.', 'success');
      setTimeout(()=> setStep(3), 280);
    };
  }

  function renderStep3(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step3');
    if (!wrap) return;

    if (!state.primaryKey || !state.plan) {
      wrap.innerHTML = '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">Choose a primary publication and renewal first.</p>';
      return;
    }

    const keys = Object.keys(PUBS).filter(k=>k!==state.primaryKey);
    if (!keys.length) {
      wrap.innerHTML = '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">No additional publications are available as add-ons.</p>';
      return;
    }

    let html = '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">Add extra subscriptions at <strong>'+ADDON_DISC+'% off</strong>. They&rsquo;ll match your renewal where available.</p>';

    keys.forEach(k=>{
      const d = PUBS[k];
      if (!d) return;
      const pid = getPlanProductId(k, state.plan);
      if (!pid) return;
      const selected = state.addOns.indexOf(k) >= 0;
      const rowSel = selected ? ' main-selected' : '';
      const prices = d.prices || {};
      const price = prices[state.plan] ? prices[state.plan] : '';
      html +=
        '<div class="wdw-pub-row'+rowSel+'" data-addon="'+k+'">' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-row-left">' +
            (d.image ? '<img src="'+d.image+'" alt="'+d.label+'">' : '') +
            '<div class="wdw-pub-row-titles">' +
              '<div class="wdw-pub-row-title-line">'+d.label+' &mdash; '+(PLAN_LABELS[state.plan] || state.plan)+'</div>' +
              (price ? '<div class="wdw-pub-row-subline">'+price+' <span style="color:#16a34a;font-weight:600;">(extra '+ADDON_DISC+'% off at checkout)</span></div>' : '') +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-row-right">' +
            '<button class="wdw-pub-btn'+(selected?' secondary':'')+'" data-addon-btn="'+k+'">'+(selected?'Remove':'Add')+'</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    });

    wrap.innerHTML = html;

    wrap.onclick = function(ev){
      const row = ev.target.closest('[data-addon]');
      const btn = ev.target.closest('[data-addon-btn]');
      const target = btn || row;
      if (!target) return;
      const k = target.getAttribute(btn ? 'data-addon-btn' : 'data-addon');
      if (!k) return;
      const idx = state.addOns.indexOf(k);
      if (idx >= 0) {
        state.addOns.splice(idx,1);
        toast('Removed '+(PUBS[k] ? PUBS[k].label : k)+' add-on.', 'info');
      } else {
        state.addOns.push(k);
        toast('Added '+(PUBS[k] ? PUBS[k].label : k)+' at '+ADDON_DISC+'% off.', 'success');
      }
      renderStep3();
    };
  }

  function renderStep4(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step4');
    if (!wrap) return;

    if (!state.primaryKey || !state.plan) {
      wrap.innerHTML = '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">Select a primary subscription and renewal first.</p>';
      return;
    }

    const allowed = 1 + state.addOns.length;
    const current = state.freeIssues.length;

    let html = '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">Pick up to <strong>'+allowed+'</strong> free issue'+(allowed>1?'s':'')+'. One per subscription. You have selected <strong>'+current+'</strong>.</p>';

    if (!FREE.length) {
      html += '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">No free issues are currently available.</p>';
      wrap.innerHTML = html;
      return;
    }

    html += '<div class="wdw-pub-free-grid">';
    FREE.forEach(item=>{
      const selected = state.freeIssues.indexOf(item.id) >= 0;
      html +=
        '<div class="wdw-pub-free-card'+(selected?' selected':'')+'" data-free-id="'+item.id+'">' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-free-card-img-wrap">' +
            (item.image ? '<img src="'+item.image+'" alt="'+(item.title||'Free issue')+'">' : '') +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-free-card-title">'+(item.title||'Free issue')+'</div>' +
          '<div class="wdw-pub-free-card-actions">' +
            '<button type="button" class="wdw-pub-btn'+(selected?' secondary':'')+'" data-free-toggle="'+item.id+'">'+(selected?'Added':'Select')+'</button>' +
            '<button type="button" class="wdw-pub-btn ghost" data-free-details="'+item.id+'">See details</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    });
    html += '</div>';

    wrap.innerHTML = html;

    wrap.onclick = function(ev){
      const detailsBtn = ev.target.closest('[data-free-details]');
      if (detailsBtn) {
        const id = parseInt(detailsBtn.getAttribute('data-free-details'), 10);
        const item = FREE.find(x=>x.id===id);
        openDescModal(item ? item.title : 'Issue details', id, { freeId:id });
        ev.stopPropagation();
        return;
      }

      const card = ev.target.closest('[data-free-id]');
      const toggleBtn = ev.target.closest('[data-free-toggle]');
      const target = toggleBtn || card;
      if (!target) return;

      const id = parseInt(target.getAttribute(toggleBtn ? 'data-free-toggle' : 'data-free-id'), 10);
      if (!id) return;
      const idx = state.freeIssues.indexOf(id);
      const allowedInner = 1 + state.addOns.length;

      if (idx >= 0) {
        state.freeIssues.splice(idx,1);
        toast('Removed free issue.', 'info');
      } else {
        if (state.freeIssues.length >= allowedInner) {
          toast('You already selected '+allowedInner+' free issue'+(allowedInner>1?'s':'')+'.', 'error');
          return;
        }
        state.freeIssues.push(id);
        toast('Added free issue ', 'success');

        if (state.freeIssues.length === allowedInner) {
          setTimeout(()=>{
            toast('You selected all your free issues &mdash; tap Review or Next to see your magic &#10024;', 'info');
          }, 600);
        }
      }
      renderStep4();
    };
  }

  function buildOrderPayload(){
    if (!state.primaryKey || !state.plan) return null;

    const items = [];

    const primaryPid = getPlanProductId(state.primaryKey, state.plan);
    if (!primaryPid) return null;
    items.push({ product_id: primaryPid, quantity: 1 });

    state.addOns.forEach(k=>{
      const pid = getPlanProductId(k, state.plan);
      if (!pid) return;
      items.push({
        product_id: pid,
        quantity: 1,
        override_mode: 'PERCENT_OFF',
        override_value: ADDON_DISC
      });
    });

    state.freeIssues.forEach(id=>{
      items.push({
        product_id: id,
        quantity: 1,
        override_mode: 'SET_PRICE',
        override_value: 0.00,
        lock_price: true,
        note: 'Free issue'
      });
    });

    return { items: items };
  }

  function renderStep5(){
    const wrap = qs('#wdw-step5');
    if (!wrap) return;

    const payload = buildOrderPayload();
    state.orderPayload = payload;

    if (!payload) {
      wrap.innerHTML = '<p class="wdw-pub-free-note">Something is missing. Please go back and complete the earlier steps.</p>';
      return;
    }

    const lines = [];
    const planLabel = PLAN_LABELS[state.plan] || state.plan;

    if (state.primaryKey && PUBS[state.primaryKey]) {
      lines.push('&bull; '+PUBS[state.primaryKey].label+' &mdash; '+planLabel);
    }
    state.addOns.forEach(k=>{
      if (!PUBS[k]) return;
      lines.push('&bull; '+PUBS[k].label+' &mdash; '+planLabel+' (with '+ADDON_DISC+'% off)');
    });

    const allowed = 1 + state.addOns.length;

    let html = '<div class="wdw-pub-review-wrap">';
    html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-title">&#10024; Making Magic&hellip;</div>';
    html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-sub">You ordered:</div>';
    html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-lines">';
    lines.forEach((txt, idx)=>{
      html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-line" style="animation-delay:'+(0.12*idx)+'s">'+txt+'</div>';
    });
    if (!lines.length) {
      html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-line" style="animation-delay:0.12s">No subscriptions selected.</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';

    html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-sub">Free issues ('+state.freeIssues.length+' of '+allowed+'):</div>';
    html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-free-grid">';
    state.freeIssues.forEach((id, idx)=>{
      const item = FREE.find(x=>x.id===id);
      if (!item) return;
      html += '<div style="animation:wdwfadeup .45s forwards ease-out '+(0.12*idx)+'s;"><img src="'+(item.image||'')+'" alt="'+(item.title||'Free issue')+'"></div>';
    });
    if (!state.freeIssues.length) {
      html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-line" style="animation-delay:0.18s">No free issues selected yet.</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';

    html += '<div class="wdw-pub-review-sub">Ready? We&rsquo;ll build your cart and then send you to checkout.</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    wrap.innerHTML = html;
  }

  function submitOrder(){
    const payload = state.orderPayload || buildOrderPayload();
    if (!payload || !payload.items || !payload.items.length) {
      toast('Please complete your selections first.', 'error');
      return;
    }

    showLoader('Adding your magic to the cart&hellip;');

    const fd = new FormData();
    fd.append('action', 'wdw_publication_add_to_cart');
    fd.append('nonce', DATA.nonce || '');
    fd.append('payload', JSON.stringify(payload));

    fetch(DATA.ajax, {
      method:'POST',
      body:fd,
      credentials:'same-origin'
    })
    .then(r=>r.json())
    .then(j=>{
      if (!j || !j.success) {
        hideLoader();
        toast((j && j.data && j.data.message) ? j.data.message : 'Unable to add items to cart.', 'error');
        return;
      }
      showLoader('&#10024; Making your cart & sending you to checkout&hellip;');
      setTimeout(()=>{
        const target = DATA.checkoutUrl || (j.data && j.data.redirect) || '/checkout-2/';
        window.location = target;
      }, 900);
    })
    .catch(()=>{
      hideLoader();
      toast('Network error. Please try again.', 'error');
    });
  }

  /* NEXT STEP BUTTON (steps 1&ndash;4 only) */
  function handleNextStep(){
    if (currentStep === 1) {
      if (!state.primaryKey) {
        toast('Pick a primary subscription to continue.', 'error');
        return;
      }
      setStep(2);
      return;
    }
    if (currentStep === 2) {
      if (!state.plan) {
        toast('Choose your renewal plan to continue.', 'error');
        return;
      }
      setStep(3);
      return;
    }
    if (currentStep === 3) {
      setStep(4);
      return;
    }
    if (currentStep === 4) {
      setStep(5);
      return;
    }
    // No Next on step 5
  }

  /* Global click handler */
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
    const t = e.target;

    /* Card click / Start Today */
    const card = t.closest('[data-pub-card]');
    if (card) {
      const key = card.getAttribute('data-pub-card');
      if (key && PUBS[key]) {
        state.primaryKey = key;
        resetState();
        toast('Building your '+PUBS[key].label+' bundle&hellip;', 'info');
        openWizard(2);
      }
      e.preventDefault();
      return;
    }

    const start = t.closest('[data-pub-start]');
    if (start) {
      const key = start.getAttribute('data-pub-start');
      if (key && PUBS[key]) {
        state.primaryKey = key;
        resetState();
        toast('Building your '+PUBS[key].label+' bundle&hellip;', 'info');
        openWizard(2);
      }
      e.preventDefault();
      return;
    }

    /* Close main modal */
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-pub-close]') || t.matches('.wdw-pub-overlay')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      closeWizard();
      return;
    }

    /* Close description modal */
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-pub-desc-close]') || t.matches('.wdw-pub-desc-overlay')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      closeDescModal();
      return;
    }

    /* Step tab click */
    const stepTab = t.closest('.wdw-pub-step');
    if (stepTab) {
      const arr = qsa('.wdw-pub-step');
      const idx = arr.indexOf(stepTab);
      if (idx >= 0) setStep(idx+1);
      e.preventDefault();
      return;
    }

    /* Submit (go to checkout) */
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-pub-submit]')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      submitOrder();
      return;
    }

    /* Go to review step */
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-pub-review]')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      setStep(5);
      return;
    }

    /* NEXT STEP (1&ndash;4 only) */
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-pub-next]')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      handleNextStep();
      return;
    }

    /* Select from description modal */
    if (t.matches('[data-wdw-pub-desc-select]')) {
      e.preventDefault();
      if (!currentDescFreeId) return;

      const allowed = 1 + state.addOns.length;
      const idx = state.freeIssues.indexOf(currentDescFreeId);

      if (idx >= 0) {
        state.freeIssues.splice(idx,1);
        toast('Removed free issue.', 'info');
      } else {
        if (state.freeIssues.length >= allowed) {
          toast('You already selected '+allowed+' free issue'+(allowed>1?'s':'')+'.', 'error');
          return;
        }
        state.freeIssues.push(currentDescFreeId);
        toast('Added free issue ','success');
        if (state.freeIssues.length === allowed) {
          setTimeout(()=>toast('You selected all your free issues &mdash; tap Review or Next to see your magic &#10024;','info'),600);
        }
      }

      const step4 = qs('#wdw-step4');
      if (step4 && step4.classList.contains('active')) {
        renderStep4();
      }
      updateDescSelectButton();
      return;
    }
  });

})();
//# sourceURL=wdw-publication-wizard-js-js-after
/* ]]> */
</script><script type="text/rlscript" id="alg-wc-ean-variations-js-extra">
