      </style><div class="wdwTPG-toast" aria-live="polite" aria-atomic="true"></div><div class="wdwTPG-overlay" aria-hidden="true"></div><div class="wdwTPG-modal" id="wdwTPG-details" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-hidden="true"><div class="wdwTPG-head"><div class="wdwTPG-headTitle">Details</div><button class="wdwTPG-close" type="button" data-wdw-tpg-close="" aria-label="Button 3">&times;</button></div><div class="wdwTPG-body"><div class="wdwTPG-gallery"></div><div class="wdwTPG-priceBig"></div><div class="wdwTPG-desc"></div><div class="wdwTPG-detailActions"></div></div><div class="wdwTPG-foot"><button class="wdwTPG-btn ghost" type="button" data-wdw-tpg-close="" aria-label="Button 4">Close</button></div></div><div class="wdwTPG-modal" id="wdwTPG-options" role="dialog" aria-modal="true" aria-hidden="true"><div class="wdwTPG-head"><div class="wdwTPG-headTitle">Choose Options</div><button class="wdwTPG-close" type="button" data-wdw-tpg-close="" aria-label="Button 5">&times;</button></div><div class="wdwTPG-body"><div class="wdwTPG-note">Pick your options, then tap <strong>Add to Cart</strong>.</div><div class="wdwTPG-optPreview"><img src="" alt="img-17"></img><div><div class="wdwTPG-optTitle"></div><div class="wdwTPG-mini" style="margin-top:4px;">Image &amp; price update when your selection matches a variation.</div></div></div><div class="wdwTPG-optionsForm"></div><div class="wdwTPG-note wdwTPG-variationMsg" style="margin-top:10px;"></div></div><div class="wdwTPG-foot"><button class="wdwTPG-btn ghost" type="button" data-wdw-tpg-close="" aria-label="Button 6">Cancel</button> <button class="wdwTPG-btn accent" type="button" data-wdw-tpg-add-variation="" disabled aria-label="Button 7">Add to Cart</button></div></div><div class="wdwTPG-lightbox" aria-hidden="true"><img alt="img-18"></img></div><script type="text/rlscript">
      (function(){
        if (window._WDW_TPG_V12) return;
        window._WDW_TPG_V12 = true;

        const AJAX  = "https://www.wdw-magazine.com/wp-admin/admin-ajax.php";
        let   NONCE = "0c6cb54893"; // now mutable so we can refresh

        const qs  = (s, el=document) => el.querySelector(s);
        const qsa = (s, el=document) => Array.from(el.querySelectorAll(s));
        const esc = (s) => String(s||'')
          .replaceAll('&','&amp;').replaceAll('<','&lt;').replaceAll('>','&gt;')
          .replaceAll('"','&quot;').replaceAll("'","&#039;");

        const TOASTS = [
          "Wish granted &mdash; adding to your cart.",
          "Rope drop energy activated.",
          "Pixie dust applied. One sec&hellip;",
          "This is giving &lsquo;best day ever&rsquo;.",
          "Popcorn bucket decisions were made.",
          "Park plan updated &mdash; cart is next.",
          "Oh boy! That&rsquo;s a good pick.",
          "Fireworks-level checkout vibes.",
          "All aboard the add-to-cart express.",
          "You&rsquo;re basically the Main Character.",
          "Making magic&hellip; don&rsquo;t move.",
          "Your cart is about to look iconic.",
          "Surprise and delight: incoming.",
          "That one&rsquo;s a classic. Great choice.",
          "Nailed it. Let&rsquo;s keep going."
        ];

        const overlay      = qs('.wdwTPG-overlay');
        const toastEl      = qs('.wdwTPG-toast');
        const modalDetails = qs('#wdwTPG-details');
        const modalOptions = qs('#wdwTPG-options');
        const lightbox     = qs('.wdwTPG-lightbox');
        const lightImg     = lightbox ? lightbox.querySelector('img') : null;

        let toastTimer = null;
        function showToast(msg){
          if(!toastEl) return;
          let text = (typeof msg === 'string') ? msg : '';
          text = text.replace(/<[^>]*>/g, '');
          toastEl.textContent = text;
          toastEl.classList.add('show');
          clearTimeout(toastTimer);
          toastTimer = setTimeout(()=> toastEl.classList.remove('show'), 2200);
        }
        function randomToast(){
          const message = TOASTS[Math.floor(Math.random()*TOASTS.length)];
          showToast(message);
        }

        function openModal(modal){
          overlay.classList.add('open');
          modal.classList.add('open');
          modal.setAttribute('aria-hidden','false');
        }
        function closeAll(){
          overlay.classList.remove('open');
          [modalDetails, modalOptions].forEach(m=>{
            m.classList.remove('open');
            m.setAttribute('aria-hidden','true');
          });
          closeLightbox();
        }
        function openLightbox(src){
          if(!lightbox || !lightImg) return;
          lightImg.src = src;
          lightbox.style.display = 'flex';
        }
        function closeLightbox(){
          if(!lightbox) return;
          lightbox.style.display = 'none';
          if(lightImg) lightImg.src = '';
        }

        // Refresh nonce if server says "Bad nonce"
        async function refreshNonce(){
          try {
            const fd = new FormData();
            fd.append('action', 'wdw_tpg_refresh_nonce');
            const res = await fetch(AJAX, {
              method: 'POST',
              body: fd,
              credentials: 'same-origin'
            });
            const json = await res.json();
            if (json && json.success && json.data && json.data.nonce) {
              NONCE = String(json.data.nonce);
              return true;
            }
          } catch (err) {
            console.error('wdwTPG: nonce refresh failed', err);
          }
          return false;
        }

        // Generic admin-ajax POST helper with optional Bad nonce auto-retry
        function post(action, data, allowRetry){
          const doRequest = () => {
            const fd = new FormData();
            fd.append('action', action);
            fd.append('nonce', NONCE);
            Object.keys(data||{}).forEach(k=>{
              const v = data[k];
              if (v instanceof File || v instanceof Blob) {
                fd.append(k, v);
              } else {
                fd.append(k, (typeof v === 'string') ? v : JSON.stringify(v));
              }
            });
            return fetch(AJAX, {
              method: 'POST',
              body: fd,
              credentials: 'same-origin'
            }).then(r => r.json());
          };

          return doRequest()
            .then(async (res) => {
              if (
                allowRetry &&
                res &&
                res.success === false &&
                res.data &&
                res.data.message === 'Bad nonce'
              ) {
                console.warn('wdwTPG: Bad nonce, attempting refresh&hellip;');
                const ok = await refreshNonce();
                if (!ok) return res;
                // retry once with new NONCE
                return doRequest().catch(() => res);
              }
              return res;
            })
            .catch((err) => {
              console.error('wdwTPG admin-ajax error', err);
              return null;
            });
        }

        // Force Woo loops into CSS grid
        function normalizeWooGrids(){
          const uls = qsa('ul.products.wdwTPG-auto');
          if (!uls.length) return;

          const vw = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth;
          let cols = 4;
          if (vw <= 520) cols = 1;
          else if (vw <= 980) cols = 2;

          uls.forEach(ul => {
            ul.style.display = 'grid';
            ul.style.gridTemplateColumns = `repeat(${cols}, minmax(0,1fr))`;
            ul.style.columnGap = '14px';
            ul.style.rowGap = '14px';
            ul.style.gridAutoFlow = 'row';
            ul.style.alignItems = 'stretch';
            ul.style.listStyle = 'none';
            ul.style.margin = '0';
            ul.style.padding = '0';

            qsa(':scope > li.product', ul).forEach(li => {
              li.style.margin = '0';
              li.style.padding = '0';
              li.style.float = 'none';
              li.style.clear = 'none';
              li.style.width = 'auto';
              li.style.maxWidth = 'none';
              li.style.minWidth = '0';
              li.style.height = '100%';
              li.style.gridColumn = 'auto';
              li.style.gridRow    = 'auto';
            });
          });
        }

        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', normalizeWooGrids);
        window.addEventListener('resize', normalizeWooGrids);

        if (window.jQuery) {
          window.jQuery(function($){
            $(document.body).on('updated_wc_div wc_fragments_refreshed', normalizeWooGrids);
            $(document).on('yith-wcan-ajax-filtered facetwp-loaded', normalizeWooGrids);
          });
        }

        // Refresh Woo fragments (mini cart etc.)
        async function refreshFragments(){
          if (typeof wc_cart_fragments_params === 'undefined') return;

          const url = wc_cart_fragments_params.wc_ajax_url
            ? wc_cart_fragments_params.wc_ajax_url.replace('%%endpoint%%', 'get_refreshed_fragments')
            : (window.location.origin + '/?wc-ajax=get_refreshed_fragments');

          const res = await fetch(url, {
            method: 'POST',
            credentials: 'same-origin'
          }).then(r => r.json()).catch(() => null);

          if (!res || !res.fragments) return;

          Object.keys(res.fragments).forEach(sel => {
            const html = res.fragments[sel];
            const node = document.querySelector(sel);
            if (node) node.outerHTML = html;
          });

          if (window.jQuery) {
            window.jQuery(document.body).trigger('wc_fragments_refreshed');
          }

          normalizeWooGrids();
        }

        /**
         * Unified add-to-cart helper
         * &#128073; We ONLY use our own admin-ajax endpoint (wdw_tpg_add_to_cart)
         * to avoid wc-ajax weirdness with variations.
         * Includes Bad nonce auto-retry.
         */
        async function wdwAjaxAddToCart(payload){
          try {
            const res = await post('wdw_tpg_add_to_cart', payload, true);
            if (!res || !res.success) {
              return { error: true, data: res || null };
            }
            return { error: false, data: res.data || {} };
          } catch (e) {
            console.error('wdwAjaxAddToCart admin-ajax exception', e);
            return { error:true };
          }
        }

        function extractErrorMessage(resObj, defaultMsg){
          let msgText = defaultMsg;

          if (!resObj || !resObj.data) return msgText;

          const data = resObj.data;

          if (data.message) {
            msgText = String(data.message);
          } else if (data.messages) {
            const tmp = document.createElement('div');
            tmp.innerHTML = data.messages;
            const txt = tmp.textContent || tmp.innerText || '';
            if (txt.trim().length) msgText = txt.trim();
          }

          return msgText;
        }

        // ---------- Details ----------
        async function openDetails(productId){
          const g = modalDetails.querySelector('.wdwTPG-gallery');
          const p = modalDetails.querySelector('.wdwTPG-priceBig');
          const d = modalDetails.querySelector('.wdwTPG-desc');
          const t = modalDetails.querySelector('.wdwTPG-headTitle');
          const actions = modalDetails.querySelector('.wdwTPG-detailActions');

          t.textContent = 'Details';
          g.innerHTML   = '';
          // Loader
          p.innerHTML   = '<span style="color:#6b7280;font-weight:900;">Loading&hellip;</span>';
          d.innerHTML   = '<p style="color:#6b7280;font-weight:900;">Loading details&hellip;</p>';
          actions.innerHTML = '';

          openModal(modalDetails);

          const res = await post('wdw_tpg_product', { product_id: String(productId) }, true).catch(()=>null);
          if(!res || !res.success){
            p.innerHTML = '';
            d.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#6b7280;font-weight:900;">Could not load details.</p>';
            return;
          }

          const data = res.data || {};
          t.textContent = data.title || 'Details';
          p.innerHTML   = data.price_html || '';

          const imgs = Array.isArray(data.images) ? data.images : [];
          g.innerHTML  = imgs.map(u=>`<img src="${esc(u)}" alt="">`).join('');
          qsa('img', g).forEach(img=>{
            img.addEventListener('click', ()=> openLightbox(img.getAttribute('src')));
          });

          d.innerHTML = data.desc || '';

          const disabledAttr = data.in_stock ? '' : ' disabled aria-disabled="true"';
          const stockNote    = data.in_stock ? '' : '<div class="wdwTPG-stock-note">Out of stock</div>';

          const viewLink = data.permalink
            ? `<a class="wdwTPG-btn ghost" href="${esc(data.permalink)}">View Product Page</a>`
            : '';

          if (data.type === 'variable') {
            actions.innerHTML = `
              <button type="button" class="wdwTPG-btn accent" data-wdw-options="${esc(data.id)}"${disabledAttr}>Options</button>
              ${viewLink}
              ${stockNote}
            `;
          } else {
            actions.innerHTML = `
              <button type="button" class="wdwTPG-btn accent" data-wdw-add="${esc(data.id)}"${disabledAttr}>Add to Cart</button>
              ${viewLink}
              ${stockNote}
            `;
          }
        }

        // ---------- Variable Options ----------
        let optionsState = {
          productId: null,
          attributes: {},
          variations: [],
          chosenVariationId: null,
          qty: 1,
          baseImg: ''
        };

        function normalizeAttrVal(v){
          return String(v || '')
            .trim()
            .toLowerCase()
            .replace(/\s+/g, '-');
        }

        function matchVariation(variations, chosenAttrs){
          const keys = Object.keys(chosenAttrs);
          if (!keys.length) return null;

          for (const v of variations){
            let ok = true;
            for (const k of keys){
              const want = normalizeAttrVal(chosenAttrs[k]);
              const gotRaw = (v.attributes || {})[k];

              if (gotRaw === '' || gotRaw === null || gotRaw === undefined) continue;

              const got = normalizeAttrVal(gotRaw);
              if (!want || !got || want !== got){ ok = false; break; }
            }
            if (ok) return v;
          }
          return null;
        }

        function fillOptionsPreviewFromCard(productId){
          const card    = document.querySelector(`.wdwTPG-card[data-pid="${productId}"]`);
          const preview = modalOptions.querySelector('.wdwTPG-optPreview');
          const imgEl   = preview ? preview.querySelector('img') : null;
          const titleEl = preview ? preview.querySelector('.wdwTPG-optTitle') : null;

          if(card){
            const t   = card.getAttribute('data-title') || '';
            const img = card.getAttribute('data-img') || '';
            optionsState.baseImg = img || '';
            if(titleEl) titleEl.textContent = t || 'This item';
            if(imgEl){
              imgEl.src = img || '';
              imgEl.style.display = img ? 'block' : 'none';
            }
          } else {
            optionsState.baseImg = '';
          }
        }

        function setOptionsPreviewImage(src){
          const preview = modalOptions.querySelector('.wdwTPG-optPreview');
          const imgEl   = preview ? preview.querySelector('img') : null;
          if(!imgEl) return;

          const finalSrc = src || optionsState.baseImg || '';
          imgEl.src = finalSrc;
          imgEl.style.display = finalSrc ? 'block' : 'none';
        }

        async function openOptions(productId){
          const t       = modalOptions.querySelector('.wdwTPG-headTitle');
          const formWrap= modalOptions.querySelector('.wdwTPG-optionsForm');
          const msg     = modalOptions.querySelector('.wdwTPG-variationMsg');
          const addBtn  = modalOptions.querySelector('[data-wdw-tpg-add-variation]');

          t.textContent = 'Choose Options';
          formWrap.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#6b7280;font-weight:900;">Loading options&hellip;</p>';
          msg.textContent = '';
          addBtn.disabled = true;
          addBtn.textContent = 'Add to Cart';

          optionsState = { productId, attributes:{}, variations:[], chosenVariationId:null, qty:1, baseImg:'' };

          fillOptionsPreviewFromCard(productId);
          openModal(modalOptions);

          const res = await post('wdw_tpg_variable', { product_id: String(productId) }, true).catch(()=>null);
          if(!res || !res.success){
            formWrap.innerHTML = '<p style="color:#6b7280;font-weight:900;">Could not load variations.</p>';
            return;
          }

          const data       = res.data || {};
          const attributes = data.attributes || {};
          const variations = Array.isArray(data.variations) ? data.variations : [];
          optionsState.variations = variations;

          let html = '';
          Object.keys(attributes).forEach(formKey=>{
            const group = attributes[formKey] || {};
            const opts  = group.options || [];
            const niceLabel = group.label || formKey.replace('attribute_','').replaceAll('_',' ');

            html += `
              <div class="wdwTPG-formRow">
                <label class="wdwTPG-label">${esc(niceLabel)}</label>
                <select class="wdwTPG-select" data-attr="${esc(formKey)}">
                  <option value="">Select&hellip;</option>
                  ${opts.map(o=>`<option value="${esc(o.value)}">${esc(o.label)}</option>`).join('')}
                </select>
              </div>
            `;
          });

          html += `
            <div class="wdwTPG-formRow">
              <div class="wdwTPG-inline">
                <div>
                  <label class="wdwTPG-label">Quantity</label>
                  <input class="wdwTPG-qty" type="number" min="1" step="1" value="1" data-qty>
                </div>
                <div>
                  <label class="wdwTPG-label">Price</label>
                  <div style="height:44px;display:flex;align-items:center;font-weight:900;border:1px solid rgba(0,0,0,.10);border-radius:14px;padding:0 12px;background:rgba(0,0,0,.03);" data-var-price>
                    Select options&hellip;
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          `;

          formWrap.innerHTML = html;

          const selects  = qsa('select[data-attr]', formWrap);
          const qtyInput = qs('[data-qty]', formWrap);
          const priceBox = qs('[data-var-price]', formWrap);

          function recalc(){
            optionsState.attributes = {};
            selects.forEach(sel=>{
              const k = sel.getAttribute('data-attr');
              const v = sel.value || '';
              if(k && v) optionsState.attributes[k] = v;
            });

            optionsState.qty = Math.max(1, parseInt(qtyInput.value || '1', 10) || 1);

            const totalAttrs  = selects.length;
            const chosenCount = Object.keys(optionsState.attributes).length;

            if (chosenCount < totalAttrs){
              optionsState.chosenVariationId = null;
              addBtn.disabled   = true;
              priceBox.textContent = 'Select options&hellip;';
              msg.textContent   = 'Choose all options to enable Add to Cart.';
              setOptionsPreviewImage(optionsState.baseImg);
              return;
            }

            const v = matchVariation(optionsState.variations, optionsState.attributes);

            if(!v){
              optionsState.chosenVariationId = null;
              addBtn.disabled   = true;
              priceBox.textContent = 'No match for that combo.';
              msg.textContent   = 'That option combo isn&rsquo;t available. Try a different selection.';
              setOptionsPreviewImage(optionsState.baseImg);
              return;
            }

            optionsState.chosenVariationId = v.variation_id;
            addBtn.disabled = !v.is_in_stock;

            if (v.price_html && String(v.price_html).trim().length){
              priceBox.innerHTML = v.price_html;
            } else if (v.display_price_formatted) {
              priceBox.textContent = v.display_price_formatted;
            } else if (v.display_price !== undefined && v.display_price !== null) {
              priceBox.textContent = String(v.display_price);
            } else {
              priceBox.textContent = '&mdash;';
            }

            msg.textContent = v.is_in_stock ? '' : 'This combination is out of stock.';

            const varImg = (v.image_full || v.image_thumb || '').trim();
            if (varImg) setOptionsPreviewImage(varImg); else setOptionsPreviewImage(optionsState.baseImg);
          }

          selects.forEach(sel=> sel.addEventListener('change', recalc));
          qtyInput.addEventListener('input', recalc);

          addBtn.onclick = async function(){
            if(!optionsState.chosenVariationId){
              showToast("Choose options first &#10024;");
              return;
            }

            addBtn.disabled = true;
            addBtn.textContent = 'Adding&hellip;';
            randomToast();

            const payload = {
              product_id:  String(optionsState.productId),
              quantity:    String(optionsState.qty),
              variation_id:String(optionsState.chosenVariationId),
              variation:   optionsState.attributes
            };

            const res2 = await wdwAjaxAddToCart(payload);
            if (!res2 || res2.error) {
              addBtn.disabled = false;
              addBtn.textContent = 'Add to Cart';

              const msgText = extractErrorMessage(res2, "Could not add to cart. Try again.");
              console.error('wdw_tpg_add_to_cart (variation) failed:', res2);
              showToast(msgText);
              return;
            }

            await refreshFragments();
            addBtn.disabled = false;
            addBtn.textContent = 'Add to Cart';
            closeAll();
            showToast("&#9989; Added to cart!");
          };

          recalc();
        }

        async function addSimple(productId, qty=1){
          const btn = document.querySelector(`[data-wdw-add="${productId}"]`);

          if (btn && (btn.disabled || btn.dataset.loading === '1')) {
            return;
          }

          if(btn){
            btn.dataset.loading = '1';
            btn.disabled = true;
            btn.textContent = 'Adding&hellip;';
          }

          randomToast();

          const res = await wdwAjaxAddToCart({
            product_id: String(productId),
            quantity:   String(qty)
          });

          if (!res || res.error) {
            if(btn){
              btn.dataset.loading = '0';
              btn.disabled = false;
              btn.textContent = 'Add to Cart';
            }

            const msgText = extractErrorMessage(res, "Couldn&rsquo;t add that &mdash; try again.");
            console.error('wdw_tpg_add_to_cart (simple) failed:', res);
            showToast(msgText);
            return;
          }

          await refreshFragments();

          if(btn){
            btn.dataset.loading = '0';
            btn.disabled = false;
            btn.textContent = 'Add to Cart';
          }
          showToast("&#9989; Added to cart!");
        }

        document.addEventListener('click', function(e){
          const det = e.target.closest('[data-wdw-details]');
          if(det){
            e.preventDefault();
            openDetails(parseInt(det.getAttribute('data-wdw-details'), 10));
            return;
          }

          const opt = e.target.closest('[data-wdw-options]');
          if(opt){
            if (opt.disabled) return;
            e.preventDefault();
            openOptions(parseInt(opt.getAttribute('data-wdw-options'), 10));
            return;
          }

          const add = e.target.closest('[data-wdw-add]');
          if(add){
            if (add.disabled) return;
            e.preventDefault();
            addSimple(parseInt(add.getAttribute('data-wdw-add'), 10), 1);
            return;
          }

          const img = e.target.closest('.wdwTPG-img');
          if(img){
            const card = e.target.closest('.wdwTPG-card');
            if(card){
              const pid = parseInt(card.getAttribute('data-pid'), 10);
              if(pid) openDetails(pid);
            }
          }

          if(e.target.matches('.wdwTPG-overlay') || e.target.closest('[data-wdw-tpg-close]')) closeAll();
          if(e.target.matches('.wdwTPG-lightbox')) closeLightbox();
        });

        document.addEventListener('keydown', (e)=>{ if(e.key === 'Escape') closeAll(); });
        if(lightbox) lightbox.addEventListener('click', closeLightbox);

      })();
